ACTOR Mastema 7265	// cyberdemon
{
	DropItem "AEoDApocalypseItem" 128
	DropItem "Mana2BigAmmo" 128
	DropItem "Mana2BigAmmo" 128
	DropItem "Mana2BigAmmo" 128
	DropItem "Mana1BigAmmo" 128
	DropItem "Mana1BigAmmo" 128
	DropItem "Mana1BigAmmo" 128
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "PowerslaveSpawner" 28
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
    Health 4000
    Radius 20
    Height 64
    Mass 1000
    Speed 8
    PainChance 32
    Monster	RipLevelMin 1
    Scale 0.38
    +BOSSDEATH
    +MISSILEEVENMORE
    +MISSILEMORE  
    +NORADIUSDMG 
    +BOSS
    +FLOORCLIP
    -FRIGHTENED
    +DONTSPLASH
    +NOICEDEATH
    +DONTMORPH
    +NOFEAR
    Obituary "%o couldn't survive Mastema's accusation."
    SeeSound "skullwizard/active"
    PainSound "skullwizard/pain"
    DeathSound "skullwizard/death"
    ActiveSound "skullwizard/active"
    AttackSound "h2necromancer/boneshot"
    MeleeDamage 9
    DamageFactor "Wormwood", 0.25
    PainChance "Drain", 40
    PainChance "Chaos", 255
    DamageFactor "ChaosExpl1", 0
    DamageFactor "ChaosExpl2", 0
//Unholy
	DamageFactor "Holy", 1.5
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "Fire", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Ice", 0.75
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.75
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 0.75
    States
    {
    Pain.Chaos:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl1",0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl2",0,0,0)
	Goto See
    Pain.Drain:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,32,0)
	Goto Pain
    Spawn:
	SWAT G 0 A_SetTranslucent(1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetShootable
        SWAI A 5 A_Look
        Goto Spawn+1
    See:
        SWAW AACCEEGG 3 A_ExtChase(0,1)
        Loop
    TeleportBack:
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Wander
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Wander
	TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("misc/teleport",7,1,0,1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TeleportFog",0,0,32,0,0,0,0,32)
	SWAT G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
  	SWAT G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.2)
	SWAT G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.3)
	SWAT G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.4)
	SWAT G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.5)
	SWAT G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.6)
	SWAT G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.7)
	SWAT G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.8)
	SWAT G 1 A_SetTranslucent(1)
	SWAT EDB 5 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetShootable
	Goto See
    Missile:
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(230,"RedRail")
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("castspell/fire")
	SWAI A 12 A_FaceTarget
        SWAB BD 5 A_FaceTarget
        SWAB F 5 A_CustomMissile("ApocalypseStarter2",40,0,0)
        SWAB G 5 A_FaceTarget
	SWAI A 10
	Goto See
    RedRail:
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"Teleport")
	SWAA ACE 4 A_FaceTarget
	SWAA G 0 A_PlaySound("h2necromancer/boneshot")
	SWAA G 0 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"00 00 00",1,5,1,"ApocPuff")
	SWAA G 3 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"Red",1,5)
	SWAA G 0 A_PlaySound("h2necromancer/boneshot")
	SWAA G 0 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"00 00 00",1,5,1,"ApocPuff")
	SWAA G 3 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"Red",1,5)
	SWAA G 0 A_PlaySound("h2necromancer/boneshot")
	SWAA G 0 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"00 00 00",1,5,1,"ApocPuff")
	SWAA G 3 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"Red",1,5)
	SWAA G 0 A_PlaySound("h2necromancer/boneshot")
	SWAA G 0 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"00 00 00",1,5,1,"ApocPuff")
	SWAA G 3 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"Red",1,5)
	SWAA G 0 A_PlaySound("h2necromancer/boneshot")
	SWAA G 0 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"00 00 00",1,5,1,"ApocPuff")
	SWAA G 3 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"Red",1,5)
	SWAA G 0 A_PlaySound("h2necromancer/boneshot")
	SWAA G 0 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"00 00 00",1,5,1,"ApocPuff")
	SWAA G 3 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"Red",1,5)
	SWAA G 0 A_PlaySound("h2necromancer/boneshot")
	SWAA G 0 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"00 00 00",1,5,1,"ApocPuff")
	SWAA G 3 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"Red",1,5)
	SWAA G 0 A_PlaySound("h2necromancer/boneshot")
	SWAA G 0 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"00 00 00",1,5,1,"ApocPuff")
	SWAA G 3 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"Red",1,5)
	SWAA G 0 A_PlaySound("h2necromancer/boneshot")
	SWAA G 0 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"00 00 00",1,5,1,"ApocPuff")
	SWAA G 3 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"Red",1,5)
	SWAA G 0 A_PlaySound("h2necromancer/boneshot")
	SWAA G 0 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"00 00 00",1,5,1,"ApocPuff")
	SWAA G 3 A_CustomRailgun(8,0,none,"Red",1,5)
	SWAA G 3 A_FaceTarget
	SWAA I 5
        Goto See
    Teleport:
	TNT1 A 0 A_UnSetShootable
	SWAT BDE 4 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("misc/teleport",7,1,0,1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TeleportFog",0,0,32,0,0,0,0,32)
	SWAT G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.8)
	SWAT G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.7)
	SWAT G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.6)
	SWAT G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.5)
	SWAT G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.4)
	SWAT G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.3)
	SWAT G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.2)
	SWAT G 1 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
	Goto "TeleportBack"
    Pain:
        SWAP D 4
        SWAP E 4 A_Pain
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(90,"Teleport")
        Goto See
    Death:
        SWAD A 3 A_Scream
	SWAD BCDEF 3
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("SWSkull",60,0,180)
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("SWBook",45,10,-90)
        SWAD G 3 A_Fall
        SWAD HIJKLMN 3
		"####" "#" 0 A_QueueCorpse
        SWAD O -1 A_KillMaster
        Stop
    Death.UnholyDisint:
    Death.PlasmaDisint:
    Disintegrate:
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_SetTranslation(0,50)	
	TNT1 a 0 A_KillMaster
	SWAP D 1 A_FadeOut(0.015)
	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
	TNT1 a 0 A_Stop	
	TNT1 a 0 A_Fall
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateShadowMediumBig",0,0,40,0,0,0,0,32)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateSparksMediumBig",0,0,40,0,0,0,0,32)
	SWAP DD 2 A_FadeOut(0.03)
	Goto Disintegrate+7
    Ice:
	"####" "#" 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
	"####" "#" 0 A_KillMaster
	"####" "#" 1 A_FreezeDeathChunks
	Wait
    }
}

	Loop

	Stop
    }
}

Actor NovaLightningFingerND
{
	var int user_failsafe;
	var int user_count;
	var int user_vel[3];
	Projectile
	+THRUACTORS
	+DONTSPLASH
	+FORCERADIUSDMG
	+EXTREMEDEATH
	+PAINLESS
	DamageType "Electric"
	Radius 4
	Height 4
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0
		//TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(128,10,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("Thunderstorm/lightning")
	Velocity:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_Explode(3,16,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_count",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_vel",0,frandom(0.75,2.0))
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_vel",1,frandom(-3.0,3.0))
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserArray("user_vel",2,frandom(-3.0,3.0))
	Warping:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("NovaLightningFingerTrail",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,0,33)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,1,2)
		TNT1 A 0 A_Warp(AAPTR_DEFAULT,user_vel[0],user_vel[1]*frandom(1.0,3.0),user_vel[2]*frandom(1.0,3.0),0,WARPF_STOP,1)
		Goto Death
		TNT1 A 0 A_Warp(AAPTR_DEFAULT,user_vel[0],user_vel[1]*frandom(1.0,3.0),user_vel[2]*frandom(1.0,3.0),0,0,"Warp2")
		Goto Death
	Warp2:
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_failsafe",user_failsafe+1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_failsafe>=3000,"Death")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_count",user_count+1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_count>=random(3,10),"Velocity")
		Loop
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 
		Stop
	}
}

ACTOR FForceCube 7280		//lost soul
{
	DropItem "Mana1Ammo"
	DropItem "PowerslaveSpawner" 32
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
    Radius 18
    Height 46
    Speed 10
    Health 60
    Mass 1000
    Monster	RipLevelMin 1
    +BOSSDEATH
    +NOGRAVITY
    +SPAWNFLOAT
    +FLOAT
    BloodType NoBloodPuff
    +DONTFALL
    +NOBLOCKMONST
    +NOICEDEATH
    +DONTMORPH
    +NOFEAR
    Obituary "%o was neutralized by a force cube."
    Scale 0.4
    maxtargetrange 160
    PainChance "Charm", 255
    PainChance "Terror", 255
    PainChance "Drain", 160
    PainChance "Chaos", 255
    PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 255
    PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 255
//Armor
	DamageFactor "Electric", 1.25
	DamageFactor "Plasma", 0.75
	DamageFactor "PlasmaDisint", 0.75
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.5
    States
    {
    Pain.Chaos:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl1",0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl2",0,0,0)
	Goto See
    Pain.ChaosExpl1:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_ClearTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",1)
	Goto Spawn
    Pain.ChaosExpl2:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",0)
	Goto See
    Pain.Charm:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)
	Goto See
    Pain.Terror:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
	Goto See
    Pain.Drain:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,32,0)
	Goto See
    Spawn:
	FCB3 A 3 A_Look
	Loop
    See:
	FCB3 A 0 A_StopSoundEx("Voice")
	FCB3 A 3 A_Chase
	Goto See+1
    Missile:
	FCB3 A 1 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("ForceCube/Fire","Voice",1,0)
	FCB3 A 2 A_CustomRailgun(random(0,1),0,none,"EB DB 57",1,1,0)
	FCB3 A 0 A_CustomRailgun(0,0,none,"C3 9B 2F",1,1,0)
	FCB3 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(256,1)
	Goto See
	FCB3 A 0 A_SpidReFire
	Goto Missile+2
    Death:
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("KESSmallExplosion",8,0,0)

	IM3W A 0 A_SentinelBob
	IM3W ABCDE 3 A_Chase
	IM3W F 0 A_SentinelBob
	IM1W F 0 A_PlaySound("hx2imp/wingflap1")
	IM3W EGHIJ 3 A_Chase
	Loop
	IM3E A 0 A_TakeInventory("ImpCharge",1)
	IM3E ABCDE 3
	Loop
    Melee:
	IM3A ABCDEFGH 2 A_FaceTarget
	IM3A I 2 A_MeleeAttack
	IM3A J 2 
	Goto See
    Missile:
	IM3B A 0 A_Jump(64,"Charge")
	IM3A ABCDEFGH 2 A_FaceTarget
	IM3A I 0 A_PlaySound("hx2imp/iceshot")
	IM3A I 2 A_CustomMissile("IceImpShot",16,0,0)
	IM3A J 2
	Goto See
    Charge:
	IM3B A 0 A_PlaySound("hx2imp/charge")
	IM3B A 0 A_GiveInventory("ImpCharge",1)
	IM3B ABCDEFGHI 2 A_FaceTarget
	IM3C A 0 A_SkullAttack(22)
	IM3C AAAAA 1 A_CustomMeleeAttack(1,"h2golem/hit","None","Normal",0)
	IM3C B 0 A_SkullAttack(22)
	IM3C BBBBB 1 A_CustomMeleeAttack(1,"h2golem/hit","None","Normal",0)
	Goto Charge+10
    Pain:
	IM3A A 0 A_TakeInventory("ImpCharge",1)
	IM3A A 2 A_Pain
	IM3A BCBA 3
	Goto See
    Death:
	IM3D B 2 A_Scream
	IM3D C 2 A_NoBlocking
	IM3D DEFGHIJKLM 2
	IM3D N -1
	Stop
    XDeath:
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0)
	TNT1 AAA 0 A_TossGib
	TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
	Stop
    Death.UnholyDisint:
    Death.PlasmaDisint:
    Disintegrate:
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_SetTranslation(0,50)	
	IM3A A 1 A_FadeOut(0.015)
	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
	TNT1 a 0 A_Stop	
	TNT1 a 0 A_Fall
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateShadowSmallMedium",0,0,18,0,0,0,0,32)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateSparksSmallMedium",0,0,18,0,0,0,0,32)
	IM3A AA 2 A_FadeOut(0.03)
	Goto Disintegrate+6
    Raise:
	IM3D MLKJIHGFEDCBA 2
	Goto See
    }
}

ACTOR ImpLord		// pain elemental
{
	DropItem "Mana2BigAmmo"
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "PowerslaveSpawner" 28
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 64
    Health 600
    Radius 30
    Height 64
    Mass 1500
    Speed 11
    PainChance 50
    Scale 0.5
    Monster	RipLevelMin 1
    +FLOORCLIP
    +FLOAT
    +NOGRAVITY
    +MISSILEMORE
    MeleeDamage 7
    MeleeSound "h2golem/hit"
    SeeSound "hx2imp/active2"
    DeathSound "hx2imp/death2"
    ActiveSound "hx2imp/active2"
    Obituary "%o was shellacked by an imp lord."
    PainChance "Charm", 192
    PainChance "Terror", 192
    PainChance "Drain", 128
    PainChance "Chaos", 255
    PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 128
    PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 128
//Undead
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 1.5
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.25
    States
    {
    Pain.Chaos:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl1",0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl2",0,0,0)
	Goto See
    Pain.ChaosExpl1:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_ClearTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",1)
	Goto Spawn
    Pain.ChaosExpl2:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",0)
	Goto See
    Pain.Charm:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)
	Goto See
    Pain.Terror:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
	Goto See
    Pain.Drain:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,32,0)
	Goto Pain
	
    Spawn:
	IM2W ABCDEFGHIJ 3 A_Look
	Loop
    See:
	IM2W A 0 A_SentinelBob
	IM2W ABCDE 3 A_Chase
	IM2W F 0 A_SentinelBob
	IM2W A 0 A_PlaySound("hx2imp/wingflap2")
	IM2W EGHIJ 3 A_Chase
	Loop
	IM2E ABCDE 3
	Loop
    Melee:
	IM2A ABCDEFGH 3 A_FaceTarget
	IM2A I 3 A_MeleeAttack
	IM2A J 3 
	Goto See
    Missile:
	IM2A ABCDEFGH 2 A_FaceTarget
	IM2A I 0 A_Jump(192,4,14)
	IM2A I 0 A_PlaySound("FighterHammerMiss")
	IM2A I 2 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordSpawner",16,0,random(-5,5))
	IM2A J 2
	Goto See
	IM3A I 0 A_PlaySound("hx2imp/fireshot")
	IM2A I 0 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordFireShot",16,0,random(-4,4))
	IM2A I 0 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordFireShot",16,0,random(-4,4))
	IM2A I 0 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordFireShot",16,0,random(-4,4))
	IM2A I 0 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordFireShot",16,0,random(-4,4))
	IM2A I 0 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordFireShot",16,0,random(-4,4))
	IM2A I 0 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordFireShot",16,0,random(-4,4))
	IM2A I 0 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordFireShot",16,0,random(-4,4))
	IM2A I 2 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordFireShot",16,0,random(-4,4))
	IM2A J 2 
	Goto See
	IM3A I 0 A_PlaySound("hx2imp/iceshot")
	IM2A I 0 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordIceShot",16,0,random(-4,4))
	IM2A I 0 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordIceShot",16,0,random(-4,4))
	IM2A I 0 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordIceShot",16,0,random(-4,4))
	IM2A I 0 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordIceShot",16,0,random(-4,4))
	IM2A I 0 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordIceShot",16,0,random(-4,4))
	IM2A I 0 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordIceShot",16,0,random(-4,4))
	IM2A I 0 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordIceShot",16,0,random(-4,4))
	IM2A I 2 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordIceShot",16,0,random(-4,4))
	IM2A J 2
	Goto See
    Pain:
	IM2A A 2 A_Pain
	IM2A BCBA 3
	IM2A A 0 A_Jump(128,1)
	Goto See
	IM2A ABCDEFGH 2 A_FaceTarget
	IM2A I 2 A_CustomMissile("ImpLordSpawner",16,0,random(-5,5))
	IM2A J 2
	Goto See
    Death.UnholyDisint:
    Death.PlasmaDisint:

	TNT1 A 0 Thing_SetTranslation(0,50)	
	IM2A A 1 A_FadeOut(0.015)
	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
	TNT1 a 0 A_Stop

	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateShadowMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,32)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateSparksMedium",0,0,30,0,0,0,0,32)
	IM2A AA 2 A_FadeOut(0.03)
	Goto Disintegrate+6
    Death:
	IM2D B 2 A_Scream
	IM2D C 2 A_NoBlocking
	IM2D DEFGHIJKLM 2
	IM2D N -1
	Stop
    XDeath:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"Death")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"XDeathBlood")
        IM2D A 4 A_Scream
	TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_TossGib
        IM2D B 2 A_NoBlocking
        IM2D CDEFGHIJKLM 2

        IM2D N -1
        Stop
    XDeathBlood:

	TNT1 AAA 0 A_TossGib
	TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
	Stop
    Raise:
	IM2D MLKJIHGFEDCBA 2
	Goto See
    }
}

ACTOR MummyLord		// baron

	DropItem "Mana2BigAmmo"
	DropItem "DarkMana"

	DropItem "PowerslaveSpawner" 28
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
    Health 1900
    Radius 22
    Height 64
    Mass 52000
    Speed 4
    PainChance 32
    Monster	RipLevelMin 1
    Scale 0.34
    +DONTMORPH
    +FLOORCLIP
    +BOSS
    MeleeDamage 6
    MeleeSound "h2golem/hit"
    SeeSound "hx2mummy/sight"
    DeathSound "hx2mummy/death"
    PainSound "hx2mummy/pain"
    ActiveSound "hx2mummy/idle"
    Obituary "%o succumbed to the curse of the mummy lord."
    PainChance "Charm", 96
    PainChance "Terror", 96
    PainChance "Drain", 64
    PainChance "Chaos", 255
    PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 128
    PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 128
//Undead
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 1.5
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.25
    States
    {
    Pain.Chaos:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl1",0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl2",0,0,0)
	Goto See
    Pain.ChaosExpl1:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_ClearTarget

	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Arm1DamageCheck",1,"SpawnMedium")
	M1FA A 3 A_Look
	Loop
    SpawnLow:
	M1LM A 3 A_Look
	Loop
    SpawnMedium:

	Loop
    See:

	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Arm1DamageCheck",1,"SeeMedium")

	M1FW CC 6 A_VileChase
	M1FW EEFFGG 4 A_VileChase
	Loop
    Missile:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Arm1DamageCheck",1,"MissileMedium")	//in theory this check isnt needed, but just in case
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(160,"MissileStaff","ScarabStaff")
	M1FA ABC 3 A_FaceTarget
	M1FA D 0 A_PlaySound("h2paladin/purifiershot")
	M1FA D 5 A_CustomMissile("Mummy1PoisonShot",32,-10,random(-3,3))
	M1FA C 5 A_FaceTarget
	M1FA D 0 A_PlaySound("h2paladin/purifiershot")
	M1FA D 5 A_CustomMissile("Mummy1PoisonShot",32,-10,random(-3,3))
	M1FA C 5 A_FaceTarget
	M1FA D 0 A_PlaySound("h2paladin/purifiershot")
	M1FA D 5 A_CustomMissile("Mummy1PoisonShot",32,-10,random(-3,3))
	M1FA C 5 A_FaceTarget
	M1FA D 0 A_PlaySound("h2paladin/purifiershot")
	M1FA D 5 A_CustomMissile("Mummy1PoisonShot",32,-10,random(-3,3))
	M1FA C 5 A_FaceTarget
	M1FA D 0 A_PlaySound("h2paladin/purifiershot")
	M1FA D 5 A_CustomMissile("Mummy1PoisonShot",32,-10,random(-3,3))
	M1FA C 5 A_FaceTarget
	M1FA D 0 A_PlaySound("h2paladin/purifiershot")
	M1FA D 5 A_CustomMissile("Mummy1PoisonShot",32,-10,random(-3,3))
	M1FA C 5 A_FaceTarget
	M1FA D 0 A_PlaySound("h2paladin/purifiershot")
	M1FA D 5 A_CustomMissile("Mummy1PoisonShot",32,-10,random(-3,3))
	M1FA C 5 A_FaceTarget
	M1FA D 0 A_PlaySound("h2paladin/purifiershot")
	M1FA D 5 A_CustomMissile("Mummy1PoisonShot",32,-10,random(-3,3))
	M1FA CBA 3 A_FaceTarget
	Goto See
    ScarabStaff:

	M1FA D 5 A_CustomRailgun(0,0,none,"4B 37 1B",1,1)

    Pain:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(600,"PainBothArms")		//If weak enough, it'll loose the right arm (with staff)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(1600,2)				//It should lose the left arm first
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,5)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Arm1DamageCheck",1,"SeeMedium")	//check first if it havent lost already the arm
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Arm1DamageCheck",1)			//If it havent lost it, here will, giving the appropiate check
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("hx2mummy/limb")
	M1MW A 0 A_CustomMissile("MummyLeftArm",40,9,135)
	TNT1 A 0 
	Goto See
    PainBothArms:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Arm2DamageCheck",1,"See")		//if already have lost the right arm, will go directly to "painfake"
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Arm1DamageCheck",1,5)			//if it have lost left arm, will directly loose the right arm
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("hx2mummy/limb")
	M1MW A 0 A_CustomMissile("MummyLeftArm",40,9,135)	//if not, will loose both here
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Arm2DamageCheck",1)		
	M1MW A 0 A_CustomMissile("MummyRightArm",40,-9,225)	
	Goto "SeeLow"
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Arm2DamageCheck",1)				//here only loses the right arm
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("hx2mummy/limb")
	MUMW A 0 A_CustomMissile("MummyRightArm",40,-9,225)	
	Goto "SeeLow"
    Death:
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("hx2mummy/fall")
	M1LD A 0 A_SpawnItem("MummyBodyDummy",0)
	M1MW A 0 A_CustomMissile("MummyLeg",20,9,225)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Arm1DamageCheck",1,2)	//check if it have lost arms
	M1MW A 0 A_CustomMissile("MummyLeftArm",40,9,135)
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Arm1DamageCheck",1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Arm2DamageCheck",1,2)
	M1MW A 0 A_CustomMissile("MummyRightArm",40,-9,225)	
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("Arm2DamageCheck",1)
	M1LD A 3
	M1LD B 3 A_Scream
	M1LD C 3 A_NoBlocking
	M1LD DEFG 3
	M1LD H 3
	TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster		//in e1m8 will perform the action there. it wasnt worth the trouble to wait until you kill the crawling version -dbt
	M1LD H 0 A_SpawnItemEx("MummyCrawler",0,0,0,0,0,0,1,32)
	Stop
	Death.Telefrag:
	Death.Massacre:
		TNT1 C 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Fall
		TNT1 A 0 A_DropItem("AEoDScarabStaffItem",1,32) //Make it so. *PICARD FAEC!11*
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,1)
		TNT1 AAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster
		Stop
	Ice:
		"####" "#" 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
		"####" "#" 0 A_KillMaster
		"####" "#" 1 A_FreezeDeathChunks
		Wait
    }
}

Actor MummyCrawler
{
	DropItem "AEoDScarabStaffItem" 32
    Monster	RipLevelMin 1
    Radius 19
    Height 32
    Mass 700
    PainChance 200
    Speed 3
    MeleeDamage 2
    Health 200
    Scale 0.34
    MeleeRange 32
    +LOOKALLAROUND
    +DONTMORPH
    +FLOORCLIP
    +BOSS
    +BOSSDEATH
    Obituary "%o was escorted to the underworld by a mummy lord."
    MeleeSound "hx2mummy/bite"
    ActiveSound "hx2mummy/idle"
    PainChance "Charm", 96
    PainChance "Terror", 96
    PainChance "Drain", 64
    PainChance "Chaos", 255
    PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 128
    PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 128
//Undead
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.75
	DamageFactor "Holy", 1.5
	DamageFactor "Unholy", 0.5
	DamageFactor "UnholyDisint", 0.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.25
    States
    {
    Pain.Chaos:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl1",0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl2",0,0,0)
	Goto See
    Pain.ChaosExpl1:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_ClearTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",1)
	Goto Spawn
    Pain.ChaosExpl2:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("QUICKTORETALIATE",0)
	Goto See
    Pain.Charm:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)
	Goto See
    Pain.Terror:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
	Goto See
    Pain.Drain:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,32,0)
	Goto Pain
    Spawn:
	M1LD H 3 A_Look
	Loop
    See:
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("hx2mummy/crawl","SoundSlot6")
	M1LC ABCDEFGHIJ 3 A_Chase
	Loop
    Melee:
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(127,"Melee2","Melee3")
	TNT1 A 0 A_MeleeAttack
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("hx2mummy/crawl","SoundSlot6")
	M1LC ABCD 3 A_ExtChase(0,0)
	M1LC EFG 3 A_ExtChase(0,0)
	M1LC HIJ 3 A_ExtChase(0,0)
	Goto See
    Melee2:
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("hx2mummy/crawl","SoundSlot6")
	M1LC ABCD 3 A_ExtChase(0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_MeleeAttack
	M1LC EFG 3 A_ExtChase(0,0)
	M1LC HIJ 3 A_ExtChase(0,0)
	Goto See
    Melee3:
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("hx2mummy/crawl","SoundSlot6")
	M1LC ABCD 3 A_ExtChase(0,0)
	M1LC EFG 3 A_ExtChase(0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_MeleeAttack
	M1LC HIJ 3 A_ExtChase(0,0)
	Goto See
    Pain:
	M1LC A 5 A_Pain
	Goto See
    Death:
	TNT1 A 0
   	TNT1 C 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Fall
	TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,1)
	TNT1 AAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("QuakeSmallGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0,1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster
	Stop
    Death.UnholyDisint:
    Death.PlasmaDisint:
    Disintegrate:
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_SetTranslation(0,50)	
	M1LC A 1 A_FadeOut(0.015)
	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
	TNT1 a 0 A_Stop	
	TNT1 a 0 A_Fall
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateShadowSmallMedium",0,0,18,0,0,0,0,32)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrateSparksSmallMedium",0,0,18,0,0,0,0,32)
	M1LC AA 2 A_FadeOut(0.03)
	Goto Disintegrate+6
    }
}

Actor Pestilence		// spider mastermind
{
	DropItem "AEoDArbalestItem"
    Monster	RipLevelMin 1
    Health 10000
    Speed 15
    Radius 40
    Height 75
    Mass 80000
    Scale 0.45
    +MISSILEEVENMORE
    +LOOKALLAROUND
    +DONTHURTSPECIES
    +NORADIUSDMG
    +BOSS
    +BOSSDEATH
    +DONTMORPH
    +NOFEAR
    +NOICEDEATH
    MeleeDamage 20
    MeleeRange 150
    Species "Pestilence"
    DamageFactor "Wormwood", 0.25
    Painchance 0
    //DropItem AEoDArbalestItem
    SeeSound "pestilence/sight"
    DeathSound "pestilence/death"
    ActiveSound "pestilence/active"
    Obituary "%o was eaten away by the grievous plagues of Pestilence."
    HitObituary "%o was stricken by Pestilence."
    PainChance "Drain", 40
    PainChance "Chaos", 255
    DamageFactor "ChaosExpl1", 0
    DamageFactor "ChaosExpl2", 0
    States
    {
    Pain.Chaos:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl1",0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("ChaosExpl2",0,0,0)
	Goto See
    Pain.Drain:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,32,0)
	Goto See
    Spawn:
	PESA A 3 A_Look
	Loop
    See:
	PESR A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	PESR A 0 A_Stop
	PESR A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PestilenceCharge",1,2)
	PESR A 0 A_Jump(256,5)
	PESR A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(120,2)
	PESR A 0 A_Jump(256,3)
	PESR A 0 A_PlaySound("h2golem/hit")
	PESR A 3 A_MeleeAttack
	PESR A 0 A_TakeInventory("PestilenceCharge",1)
	PESR A 0 A_TakeInventory("PestilenceChargeLoop",7)
	PESW ABCDEF 4 A_ExtChase(0,1)	//Normal chase, to reach the missile state
	PESW Z 0 A_PlaySound("clop")
	PESW GHIJKL 4 A_ExtChase(0,1)
	PESW Z 0 A_PlaySound("clop")
	Loop
    Missile:
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetShootable
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(400,"Charge")
	TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"Arbalest","Summon","Charge","Nova")
    Charge:
	PESR A 0 A_Jump(96,1)
	Goto Missile+2
	PESR A 10 A_FaceTarget
	PESR A 0 A_SetInvulnerable
	PESR A 0 A_GiveInventory("PestilenceCharge",1)
	PESR A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("PestilenceChargeLoop",7,"See")
	PESR A 0 A_CustomMissile("HellRootS2T1", 0, -16, 0)
	PESR A 0 A_FaceTarget
	PESR A 0 A_PlaySound("eidolon/stomp",CHAN_VOICE,0.6,0)
	PESR A 1 A_Recoil(-2.2)
	PESR A 0 A_JumpIf(momx==0,2)
	PESR A 0 A_Jump(256,2)
	PESR A 0 A_JumpIf(momy==0,"See")
	PESR A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(70,"See")
	PESR A 0 A_FaceTarget
	PESR A 1 A_Recoil(-2.2)
	PESR A 0 A_JumpIf(momx==0,2)
	PESR A 0 A_Jump(256,2)
	PESR A 0 A_JumpIf(momy==0,"See")
	PESR A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(70,"See")
	PESR A 0 A_FaceTarget
	PESR A 1 A_Recoil(-2.2)
	PESR A 0 A_JumpIf(momx==0,2)
	PESR A 0 A_Jump(256,2)
	PESR A 0 A_JumpIf(momy==0,"See")
	PESR A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(70,"See")
	PESR B 0 A_CustomMissile("HellRootS2T1", 0, 16, 0)
	PESR B 0 A_FaceTarget
	PESR B 1 A_Recoil(-2.2)
	PESR B 0 A_JumpIf(momx==0,2)
	PESR B 0 A_Jump(256,2)
	PESR B 0 A_JumpIf(momy==0,"See")
	PESR B 0 A_JumpIfCloser(70,"See")
	PESR B 0 A_FaceTarget
	PESR B 1 A_Recoil(-2.2)
	PESR B 0 A_JumpIf(momx==0,2)
	PESR B 0 A_Jump(256,2)
	PESR B 0 A_JumpIf(momy==0,"See")
	PESR B 0 A_JumpIfCloser(70,"See")
	PESR B 0 A_FaceTarget
	PESR B 1 A_Recoil(-2.2)
	PESR B 0 A_JumpIf(momx==0,2)
